RTZOM PAS PHYOGS MTHAR SPEL BA DANG , ,MI NUB BSTAN PA'I RGYAL
MTSAN BSGRENG BAR SHOG ,PHYOGS KYI 'KHOR LO'I 'JIG RTEN SPYI
SGOS SU, ,MI MTHUN RGUD MUN SEL BA'I NYI MA DANG , PHAN BDE MI
ZAD 'BYUNG BA'I YID BZHIN NOR, ,DGE MTSAN RGYUN

CHAD MED PA'I GTER DU SHOG ,'DZAM GLING YANGS PA'I MTHA' DBUS
RGYAL KHAMS SU, ,DGE LEGS GRU CHAR 'BEBS PA'I GZHI DANG RTEN,
,PHYAG NA PAD MO'I CHOS SRID RAB BRTAN CING, ,'PHRIN LAS 'CHAR
NUB BRAL BAR RTAG 'PHEL SHOG ,YANG SGOS THEG CHEN CHOS KYI SDE
CHEN PO, ,RMAD BYUNG THOS BSAM NOR GLING 'DUS

BA'I GRAW, SDOM BRTZON BLO GSAL MKHAS MANG RTAG 'DU ZHING ,
,CHOS 'BYOR THUGS MTHUN DGA' STON RGYAS PAR SHOG ,'CHAD RTZOD
RTZOM PA'I DBYAR RNGA RTAG SGROG CING , ,TSUL GNAS THOS BSAM
BSGOM PA'I CHAR RGYUN 'PHEL, ,BSTAN 'GRO'I PHAN BDE LEGS TSOGS
GYEN 'DEGS PA'I, ,MKHAS BTZUN DBYAR GYI LANG TSO DOMS

@55B PAR SHOG ,MI ZAD CHOS SBYIN PAR GYI DGE RGYUN GZHIR, ,'BREL
THOGS SPYI DANG MCHED ZLA LTOS BCAS KYI, ,SGO GSUM RNAM DKAR
THOS BSAM BSGOM PA LA, ,BAR GCOD BGEGS KYI MING YANG MED PAR
SHOG ,DBU PHAR 'DUL MDZOD TSAD MA'I GZHUNG LUGS KYI, ,RIGS LAM
THOS BSAM SGOM PA'I SNOD GYUR PA'I, ,RTEN BZANG

RIM PAR BRGYUD LAS MDO SNGAGS KYI, ,CHA TSANG LAM GYI BGROD PA
MTHAR PHYIN SHOG ,DER MA SON PA'I TSE RABS THAMS CAD DU, ,'JAM
DPAL SNYING PO'I BSTAN DANG MI 'BRAL ZHING, ,BSTAN 'GROR SMAN
PA'I RLABS CHEN BYA BA YI, ,DGE LEGS DPAL GYIS SRID MTHAR SKYONG
NUS SHOG ,MDOR NA DENG NAS TSE RABS THAMS CAD DU,,

LEGS BYAS DRI MED SGO GSUM RTAG GUS KYIS, ,DRIN CAN BLA MA YAB
SRAS DGYES PA YI, ,MCHOD SPRIN NAM MKHA'I KHAMS GNAS SPRO BAR
SHOG ,DUS SKABS KUN DU MCHOG GSUM LHA TSOGS DANG , ,MYUR MDZAD
MGON PO DAM CAN GSHIN RJE'I RGYAL, ,RNAM MANG THOS SRAS DMAG ZOR
LHA MO YIS, ,BSRUNG SKYOB 'PHRIN LAS

RNAM BZHIS RTAG SKYONG SHOG ,KHYAD PAR THEG CHEN CHOS GRA SPYI
SGOS KYI, ,BSRUNG MA'I BYED POR SNGON GYI G-YAR DAM CAN, ,BEG
TZE THA 'OG RGYAL CHEN 'KHOR BCAS KYIS, ,RTAG TU SKYONG BA'I
'PHRIN LAS MA G-YAL MDZOD, ,JI SRID GLING BZHIR NYI ZLA'I BGROD
PA YIS, ,SPYI SGOS MUN STUG SEL BA DE SRID DU, ,LEGS BSHAD 'DIS

KYANG MTHA' DBUS GZHIR GNAS PA'I, ,THAR 'DOD YONGS KYI RGUD MUN
SEL GYUR CIG , (CES GANGS RI'I KHROD KYI MKHAS MANG RGYU SKAR
GYI 'PHRENG BA DBYINGS SU 'GEBS PA'I NGES PA DON GYI MKHAS GRUB
SMRA BA'I NYI MA RJE BTZUN CHOS KYI RJE BSTAN DAR BA CHEN PO'I
GSUNG RGYUN PAD MA'I TSAL RAB LAS BSTAN BCOS MNGON PAR RTOGS
PA'I RGYAN 'GREL BA DANG BCAS PA'I MTHA' DPYOD LEGS)

(PAR BSHAD PA PAD MA DKAR BO'I 'PHRENG BA ZHES BYA BA 'DI NYID
SER SMAD THOS BSAM NOR BU'I GLING DU RGYUN GTAN RTZIS BZHAG DU
BTANG BA'I PHAR PHYIN GYI 'CHAD NYAN RKANG TSUGS PA'I MKHAS GRUB
BYE BA'I BSTI GNAS SU GYUR PA LAS SNGA SOR 'DI PHYOGS SU BAR LAM
'KHOD CING, GRWA TSANG KHAM TSAN SO SOR MTHA' DPYOD 'DI'I BRIS
MA'I DPE RGYUN MANG TSAM BYUNG 'DUG NA'ANG, PHYIS 'DUS TSOGS
RGYAS SHING YIG CHA 'DI RIGS YUL)

(DUS KYIS BDRI RTZOM BGYID PA'I YON MCHOD RTEN 'BREL 'DZOM DKA'
BAS, DPE RGYUN SPEL MKHAN NYUNG STABS, SLOB GNYER BA RNAMS LA
'DZIN DPE DKON PAR YOD GSHIS, LDU MAR BA'I YAB RJE RDO RJE TSE
RING NAS RNAM DKAR THUGS BZHED CHEN POS CHOS SBYIN RGYA CHER
SPEL SLAD DU 'DI'I PAR GSAR BRKOS KYI MTHUN RKYEN SBYOR GNANG
THOG ,MTHA' DPYOD 'DI NYID SNGA SOR MKHAS GRUB CHEN PO DE NYID
KYIS BLO THOG NUS)

(@56A *, ,RTZIS BZHAG TU GNANG BSLOB MA RNAMS KYIS ZIN BRIS SU
BGYIS PA YID ZHES NGAG BRGYUN LA 'DUG PA LTAR YIN NAM, ? SGON
YOD KYI BRIS MA RNAMS BAR BAR DU TSIG 'PHRENG YOD MED MI 'DRA BA
BKA' RE YOD TSOD 'DUG NA'ANG, ? PAR BSKOS DUS GTUGS KYIS CHA
BSDUS MA LCOGS SHING TSIG KYANG BSDUS TSOGS CHE BA DANG BRIS NOR
RGYUN 'BYAMS MANG STABS, PHYI MOR MA RE ? )

(BAS CO NE BSHAD SGRUB GLING GI PAR MA LA GZHI BYAS YIG NOR CHAD
LHAG DANG SDEB SBYOR RNAMS, ZHAL MNGA' NAS RDA DPON SLOB BLO
BZANG THUGS RJE NAS BSNON 'BRI BZO BCOS ZHUS DAG MDZAD, STOD CHA
DANG 'BAR CHA RNAMS YIG MKHAN DBU MDZAD NYA ZLA, SMAD CHA RNAMS
DBU MDZAD NGAG DBANG RDO RJES TSUGS LEGS DKAR SNYOMS DAG PAR
BRIS, BRKOS MKHAN DBU MDZAD TSE DBANG BKRA SHIS SOGS KYIS)

(TING ZAB BCAD GTZANG BRKOS TE, GONG GSAL SBYIN DAG LAS BYAD
NAS, LHA BTZUN SPRUL SKU RIN PO CHE BLO BZANG 'JAM DPAL RAB
RGYAS DANG , SKU MCHED CHOS MDZAD BLO BZANG 'JAM DBYANG GNYIS
KYI LEGS BSHAD KYI DGA' STON DU BSKRUN TE, THOS BSAM NOR BU'I
GLING KYI BLO BSAL MKHAS MANG RGYA MTSO'I 'JUG NGOGS SU 'BUL
SBYOR GNANG BA'I BSAM SBYOR 'BREL THOGS KYI DGE TSOGS JI)

(SNYAD BSAGS PA DES, 'CHAD RTZOD RTZOM PA'I DBYAR RNGA'I SGRA
DBYANGS PHYOGS BCUR SGROG CING THOS BSAM BSGOM PA'I CHAR RGYUN
RTAG TU DBAB STE, LUS CAN KUN LA DGE LEGS DBYAR GYI LANG TSO DUS
KUN TU RGYAS PAR 'GYUR BA'I PAR BYANG SMON TSIG TU DGOS ZHAS,
GZHUNG LUGS KUN LA MKHYEN PA'I SPYAN STONG MNGA' BA, DPON SLOB
RAB 'BYAMS PA GRAGS PA MKHAS GRUB KYIS LHA RDZAS MDZOD)

(GTAGS DRI MED SOGS DNGOS PO'I GNANG SKYES DANG BCAS BSKUL MA
BYUNG BA LTAR, ` BLA MA DAM PA'I SLOB BU'I THA CHUNG DGE SLONG
NGAG DBANG BSTAN 'DZIN GYIS YUNG BA LHUN GRUB SDINGS KYI GZHIS
KHAR BRIS PA'I YI GE'I GROGS NI SDE PA 'PHRIN LAS DON GRUB KYIS
BGYIS PA, 'DIS KYANG BSTAN PA RIM PO CHE MI NUB CING 'PHEL PA'I
RGYUR GYUR CIG ,, ` ,,GANG GI BLO BROS SGRIB GNYIS SPRIN BRAL
NYI LTAR RNAM DAG RAB)

(GSAL BAS, ,JI SNYED DON KUN JI BZHIN GZIGS PHYIR NYID KYI THUGS
KAR GLEGS BAM 'DZIN, GANG DAG SRID PA'I BTZON RAR MA RIGS MUN
'THOMS SDUG BSNGAL GYIS GZIR BA'I, ,'GRO TSOGS KUN LA BU GCIG
LTAR BRTZA ? YAN LAG DRUG CU'I DBYANGS LDAN GSUNG, ,'BRUG LTAR
CHER SGROG NYON MONGS GNYID SLONG LAS KYI LCAGS SGROG 'GROL

MDZAD RAL GRI BRNAMS,,)

(GDOD NAS DAG CING SA BCU'I MTHAR SON YON TAN LHUN RDZOGS RGYAL
